Famous Malware | Malicious Software | Windows
![](https://cdn.discordapp.com/emojis/775983365584453642.png)  [GDrive] Suspected anti-piracy malware  @Unknown   @Unknown    @Unknown   @Unknown

This malware uses different techniques to gain permissions to edit the victim's "hosts" file. This results in the victim not being able to visit any of the sites added to the hosts file. This can be fixed by simply removing the added URLs from the "hosts" file.
More information about this malware can be found here:  [https://www.zdnet.com/article/this-strange-malware-stops-you-from-visiting-pirate-websites/](https://www.zdnet.com/article/this-strange-malware-stops-you-from-visiting-pirate-websites/)


If you want to extract the URLs from this malware, start up a windows VM, run this malware inside, allow it to do its thing, then check your hosts file inside the VM.


Original Pirate Bay posting:  [https://thepiratebay.org/description.php?id=47241486](https://thepiratebay.org/description.php?id=47241486)
(The post description matches the one in the article^)(The file size is also much too small to be the real program)


Virustotal: Antivirus cannot see inside a password protected archive. Also, this is malware lol.

Download text file I made with magnet link inside:  [https://drive.google.com/file/d/1DBMsJItwPoYEe6E_PHuWkB-K4krKcn8s/view?usp=sharing](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1DBMsJItwPoYEe6E_PHuWkB-K4krKcn8s/view?usp=sharing)


[This strange malware stops you from visiting pirate websites | ZDNet](https://www.zdnet.com/article/this-strange-malware-stops-you-from-visiting-pirate-websites/)


An odd vigilante campaign is preventing victims from accessing pirate content online.

Maltego is software used for open-source intelligence and forensics, developed by Paterva from Pretoria, South Africa. Maltego focuses on providing a library of transforms for discovery of data from open sources, and visualizing that information in a graph format, suitable for link analysis and data mining.
